< review>
Courteous, Professional & Efficient
May 20, 2020

I Have used Tom's for years on and off but in 2018 I bought a new set of tires for my STI. I just had the oil changed at Timon's Subaru and they wanted $30+ to rotate the tires. I had a feeling when I bought the tires from Tom's they mentioned free rotation for the life of the tires so I called out of the blue and sure enough that is a thing. A day later they had the car booked in, rotated tires and checked the breaks, which to my relief are good for another 12 months.

All this in a clean Safe, friendly environment. Everyone there was courteous and I was in and out in less than 30 mins. Hardly time to make use of the free wifi.
You expect good service when you are paying a lot of money for something, but this was all zero $ and they didn't find a single thing to say " sir we noticed this and recommend we carry out the work for you", just good old professional service, I feel like I have "a car guy who doesn't rip you off".

Great job Tom's, 5 stars!!<//review>

I took my smart fortwo here for alignment (they were recommended by Madness Autoworks). It turned out my car had more serious issues, but they were able to quickly resolve the problem after diagnosing it and even provided a rental when the repair was delayed due to wrong part sizes.
Everyone was very friendly, they went above and beyond. The waiting area has a tv, cookies, a Keurig, and a fridge with assortment of beverages. My car's steering wheel warning light came on right after I left and they were super accommodating, checking everything over to be sure the car's functioning and safe. Very satisfied with how everything turned out and would 10/10 bring my car back here again.
*Update* brought my car in after an accident that broke my wheel, and it needed many repairs. Tom's was able to diagnose and attend to my vehicle in a matter of days. I got a flat tire on Thursday and I went back to Walmart where I purchased it, to get it replaced.  First they did not have the tire in stock, so they put on my tiny spare tire, told me that they could order it, I would have it the next day and they would call me when it arrived.  Well no call came, so I called them in the late afternoon on Friday.  They said they had my tire and to come and they would put it on for me.  I arrived and waited well over an hour and they did nothing, then they came in and told me they did not have my tire, and that there were plenty of local tire shops close by where I could get another tire....really.

So I packed up my car and went on google to find a tire shop in the area.  Needless to say I was concerned because it was the end of the day and my spare is only good for 50 miles.  A whole list came up, but only one with a 5 star rating and it was Tom's Tire Pros.  I called them around 5:00 pm on a Friday, and they close at 5:30pm. This is a review for two experiences. One visit was dining in and the security and was for take-out.

<rate>5</rate>< Review>
My sister lives in Livermore, and I travel from Gilroy to go to Terre Mia's with her. It's an annual event for us and we always order the same thing: a glass of Prosecco, Carbonara, and we share a Spumoni for dessert. The Carbonara is wonderful and very authentic--not saucy at all. It's on the "dry" side but so flavorful with pancetta.  Delicious!  The Spumoni finishes the meal off nicely.<//Review>

Sadly, this place has decent reviews, but my wife and I had a horrible experience with the food. Started off with being told to sit anywhere we wanted on the patio, so we did. Two tables who were sat after us we greeted and given menus and a waiter, but 10 minutes later...we still hadn't been acknowledged so I went and told the host. 5 min after that, we were greeted. I asked the waiters recommendation on a bottle of Rose...he recommended the most expensive, but had no tasting notes to go with his rec. I asked if they had Linguini and clams. The waiter told me "no....this is not italian authentic, so we don't have that".  What a lie.  My wife ordered the fetcuini al salmon and I ordered a pesto pasta with salmon on top. We also ordered a calamari fritti to start.  Calamari came out and was soft and chewy.....no crisp at all. I sent it back telling them why. They brought it back 5 min later and they had dumped the calamari back in the oil and killed it. Now it was crispy, chewy grossness. We set it aside, not eating it. Then the pastas came....  Both were horrible. My wife pasta was under al dente, and mine was overcooked....but they were the same noodle. The Salmon was diced into small pieces and incorporated into the dish rather than a nice fillet on top. Salmon was horrible....overcooked beyond done! It tasted and smelled horrible.
After telling the waiter, the manager came over and i very very kindly explained how bad our meal was, pointing out exactly why wit the salmon and the calamari. Then our bill came. They removed my entree, but still charged me for my wife's horrible entree and the sad calamari. The only thing worth paying for was the wine. So in the end, I paid out $90.00 ($40.00 for the wine & $15.00 tip) and left hungry and annoyed. Stopped at in-n-out on the way home, which was 100 times better that Terra Mia. <review>We held our wedding reception at Terra Mia and are really glad we did! From early on, the co-owners were extremely helpful and accommodating, particularly Daniele. On the day of, we were swamped with wedding related activities, and the owners and wait staff made sure things ran smoothly with table arrangements, decorations, etc while we were absent. During service, wait staff were fantastically smooth and efficient, never in the way, but always available if we needed anything. The manager was able to quickly put together an alternative meal when it turned out one guest couldn't eat something (gorgonzola in the gnocchi). And the food was top-to-bottom great. We had the banquet options of caprese, garlic bread, osobucco, gnocchi, finished with tiramisu. All were delicious and and we heard only compliments from the guests (3/4 of whom were asian and wouldn't mind telling us if anything was wrong!). Wine and cocktail selection was excellent as well. All-in-all, Terra Mia, its owners, and its staff made our wedding reception as high quality as we could have asked, our guests happy, and us able to enjoy the evening with minimal stress. My only regret from the evening is that my brain was so fried with everything else that I think I forgot to tip as much as I wanted. I'll make it up though, next time I'm in the area as I'm sure we'll be coming back!<//review>< Rate>
